TITLE      .Double-Differential Cross Sections from Inelastic     2241000100003 
            Neutron Scattering on Elemental Lead.                 2241000100004 
COMMENT    .Elastic Scattering is not Included in Cross-Sections  2241000100005 
AUTHOR     (D.Schmidt,W.Mannhart,B.R.L.Siebert)                   2241000100006 
INSTITUTE  (2GERPTB)  PTB, Braunschweig, Germany.                 2241000100007 
FACILITY   (CYCLO,2GERPTB) Turnable CV-28 Compact Cyclotron (1 ns 2241000100008 
                   pulse width) And Multi-Angle Neutron           2241000100009 
                   Time-Of-Flight Spectrometer.                   2241000100010 
REFERENCE  (C,97TRIEST,1,407,199705) Main Ref. Proc. Int. Conf.   2241000100011 
                 NDST,  Trieste, Italy (1997), Vol.1, P.407-409   2241000100012 
           (R,INDC(GER)-43,53,1997) Progress Report INDC(GER)-043 2241000100013 
               (NEA/NSC/DOC(1997)13), (1997) 53                   2241000100014 
EXP-YEAR   (1994)     Data Measured. 199711 - Data Published      2241000100015 
DETECTOR   (SCIN) Five NE213 neutron detectors, located behind a  2241000100016 
            massive collimator shielding in a distance of 1200 cm 2241000100017 
            from the sample. Angular separation between the       2241000100018 
            detectors is 12.5 deg. Detector's diameter is 10.16   2241000100019 
            cm (DET1)/ 25.40 cm (DET2-DET5), length 2.54 cm       2241000100020 
            (DET1)/ 5.08 cm (DET2-DET5). The angle region covered 2241000100021 
            is 12.5 to 160 deg. An additional NE213 detector was  2241000100022 
            used as relative fluence monitor, diameter 3.81 cm,   2241000100023 
            length 3.81 cm. The movable monitor (in a fixed       2241000100024 
            distance of 651 cm) was always in a position of       2241000100025 
            58.9 deg. relative to the beam axis.                  2241000100026 
INC-SOURCE (D-D) Deuterium gas target, 1.0 cm in diameter and     2241000100027 
            3.0 cm in length, gas pressure 2.0 Hpa.               2241000100028 
INC-SPECT   Mean neutron energy is defined within +/- 20 keV.     2241000100029 
METHOD     (TOF) Time-of-flight, 12 m flight path.                2241000100030 
           (PSD) n/gamma discrimination with pulse shape analysis 2241000100031 
MONITOR    (1-H-1(N,EL)1-H-1,,DA) Polyethylene sample             2241000100032 
            (diameter 24.56 mm, height 49.74 mm, mass 22.46 g,    2241000100033 
            H content 14.30 %).                                   2241000100034 
SAMPLE      Elemental lead, cylindrical sample, 99.9% purity,     2241000100035 
            diameter 25.0 mm, height 50.0 mm, mass 278.26 g,      2241000100036 
            placed 17.5 cm from the gas target centre.            2241000100037 
CORRECTION .Monte Carlo simulated TOF spectra of the complete     2241000100038 
            angular distribution were iteratively adjusted to     2241000100039 
            the measured TOF spectra. The simulation comprised    2241000100040 
            the neutron production in the gas target and the      2241000100041 
            scattering geometry between target, sample and        2241000100042 
            detectors.                                            2241000100043 
            Parasitic neutrons from the D(d,np) breakup reaction  2241000100044 
            were simulated and subtracted. The data for the       2241000100045 
            simulation were adjusted by additional measurements   2241000100046 
            of the neutron scattering with a 4He(d,np) neutron    2241000100047 
            source (only breakup neutrons).                       2241000100048 
ERR-ANALYS (ERR-T)     Total errors comprise counting statistics  2241000100049 
                and systematic contributions of                   2241000100050 
           (ERR-1)     - Efficiency (2%),                         2241000100051 
           (ERR-2)     - Angle Uncert. (0.2 DEG),                 2241000100052 
           (MONIT-ERR) - n-p scattering (1%),                     2241000100053 
           (ERR-3)     - Multiple Scattering Correction (5%).     2241000100054 
           (ERR-4)   An additional uncertainty of 5% of the ratio 2241000100055 
                     n-Bu/n-In is taken into account              2241000100056 
                (N-BU = subtracted  fraction of scattered breakup 2241000100057 
                neutrons, n-In = fraction of inelastically        2241000100058 
                scattered neutrons after breakup subtraction).    2241000100059 
ANALYSIS        The double-differential inelastic cross sections  2241000100060 
                were extracted as elemental cross sections.       2241000100061 
COVARIANCE .           Complete covariance matrices of the        2241000100062 
                fitted Legendre coefficients are available upon   2241000100063 
                request from the  authors                         2241000100064 
                ( E-MAIL: DANKWART.SCHMIDT@PTB.DE ).              2241000100065
